<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усиленный.html>уси́ленный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usílennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>intensified, stronger
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:усиленный.html>уси́ленное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:питание.html>пита́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>usílennoje</b> pitánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">high-calorie diet; nourishing diet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:усиленный.html>уси́ленные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:занятие.html>заня́тия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>usílennyje</b> zanjátija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">concentrated study</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:усиленный.html>уси́ленное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдение.html>наблюде́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>usílennoje</b> nabljudénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">intensified supervision</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:усиленный.html>уси́ленные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:просьба.html>про́сьбы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>usílennyje</b> prósʹby</i> ― <span class="e-translation">earnest/urgent requests/entreaties</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***усиливаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усиливаться.html>уси́ливаться</a> (5814)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усиливать.html>уси́ливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usílivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усиливаться.html>уси́ливаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usílivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усилиться.html>уси́литься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become stronger, to intensify, to gain strength</li>
<li>to swell, to grow louder</li>
<li>to gather momentum</li>
<li>to deepen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эпидемия.html>эпиде́мия</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:усиливаться.html>уси́ливается</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">epidémija <b>usílivajetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the epidemic is gaining ground</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усиливать.html>уси́ливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usílivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"> 
</th>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"><a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a>.
</th>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF">прош.
</th>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелеть.html>повели́т</a>.

***усилиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усилиться.html>уси́литься</a> (10660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усилить.html>уси́лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usílitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усилиться.html>уси́литься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usílitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усиливаться.html>уси́ливаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become stronger, to intensify, to gain strength
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:усилиться.html>уси́лился</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">véter <b>usílilsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wind became stronger</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to swell, to grow louder</li>
<li>to gather momentum</li>
<li>to deepen</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усилить.html>уси́лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usílitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ускользать.html>ускольза́ть</a> (10734)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускользнуть.html>ускользну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uskolʹznútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускользать.html>ускольза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uskolʹzátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускользнуть.html>ускользну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to slip off, to slip away</li>
<li>to steal <i>(away)</i>, to sneak off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to escape
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ускользать.html>ускольза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> чьего́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uskolʹzátʹ</b> ot čʹjevó-libo vnimánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to escape someone's attention/notice; be overlooked by someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skolʹzítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skolʹznútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользя́щий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skolʹzjáščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скольжение.html>скольже́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skolʹžénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ускользнуть.html>ускользну́ть</a> (12609)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skolʹznútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускользнуть.html>ускользну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uskolʹznútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускользать.html>ускольза́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to slip off, to slip away</li>
<li>to steal <i>(away)</i>, to sneak off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to escape
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ускользнуть.html>ускользну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> чьего́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uskolʹznútʹ</b> ot čʹjevó-libo vnimánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to escape smb's attention/notice; be overlooked by smb</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skolʹzítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skolʹznútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользя́щий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skolʹzjáščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скольжение.html>скольже́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skolʹžénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользкий.html>ско́льзкий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skólʹzkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользкий.html>ско́льзко</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skólʹzko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорить.html>уско́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uskóritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорение.html>ускоре́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uskorénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорение.html>ускоре́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорение.html>ускоре́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорение.html>ускоре́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>acceleration (act, state)</li></ol>

<ol><li>speeded up, faster, (more) rapid

***ускорить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ускорить.html>уско́рить</a> (9058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорить.html>уско́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uskóritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорять.html>ускоря́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hasten, to quicken, to accelerate</li>
<li>to expedite, to speed up</li>
<li>to precipitate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">убыстрить</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ubystritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приблизить.html>прибли́зить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priblízitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***ускорять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ускорять.html>ускоря́ть</a> (14137)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорить.html>уско́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uskóritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорять.html>ускоря́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uskorjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорить.html>уско́рить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hasten, to quicken, to accelerate</li>
<li>to expedite, to speed up</li>
<li>to precipitate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убыстрять.html>убыстря́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ubystrjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приближать.html>приближа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">približátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скорый.html>ско́рый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skóryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорение.html>ускоре́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uskorénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорять.html>ускоря́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uskorjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ускорять.html>ускоря́ющий</a> (14137)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ускорять.html>ускоря́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uskorjájuščij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уследить.html>уследи́ть</a> (19461)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следить.html>следи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sledítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уследить.html>уследи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usledítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">усле́живать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep sight of, to watch</li>
<li>to keep one's focus on, to keep track of, to follow <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to look out for, to keep an eye on, to keep from harm <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slóvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:условие.html>усло́вие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uslóvije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:условие.html>усло́вия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:условие.html>усло́вия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:условие.html>усло́вий</a></b>)

***условиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:условиться.html>усло́виться</a> (13627)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slóvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:условиться.html>усло́виться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uslóvitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">усла́вливаться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">усло́вливаться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to arrange <i>(with, with + to)</i>, to agree <i>(with on, with + to )</i>, to settle <i>(with, with + to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:условиться.html>усло́виться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:встретиться.html>встре́титься</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uslóvitʹsja</b> vstrétitʹsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to arrange to meet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:условиться.html>усло́виться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́че</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uslóvitʹsja</b> o vstréče</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to arrange a meeting</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:условиться.html>усло́вились</a></b> бо́льше <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní <b>uslóvilisʹ</b> bólʹše ob étom ne govorítʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they agreed not to speak about it any more</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:условиться.html>усло́виться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дне</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uslóvitʹsja</b> o dne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to settle the day; fix the date; agree on the day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окончательно.html>оконча́тельно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:условиться.html>усло́виться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">núžno okončátelʹno <b>uslóvitʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">we must get it settled (once and for all)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обуславливать.html>обусла́вливать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obuslávlivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обусловить.html>обусло́вить</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obuslóvitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>усло́вный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uslóvnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>усло́вно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uslóvno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:условность.html>усло́вность</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uslóvnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***условленный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:условленный.html>усло́вленный</a> (21378)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:условие.html>усло́вие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uslóvije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:условленный.html>усло́вленный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uslóvlennyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>prearranged <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">signal, meeting place, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>agreed-upon <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">amount, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The short forms follow pattern <i>a*(2)</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:условленный.html>усло́влена</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:условленный.html>усло́влено</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:условленный.html>усло́влены</a>) per <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>Русский</a> орфографический <a href = vnd.unilang:словарь.html>слова́рь</a> and Орфографический <a href = vnd.unilang:словарь.html>слова́рь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языка́</a>, but pattern <i>a*(1)</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:условленный.html>усло́вленна</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:условленный.html>усло́вленно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:условленный.html>усло́вленны</a>) per Zaliznyak. In practice, both forms are found.</li></ul>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">усло́вленность</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uslóvlennostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***условный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>усло́вный</a> (6307)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:условие.html>усло́вие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uslóvije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>усло́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uslóvnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>conditional <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">depending upon a condition</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>усло́вная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вероятность.html>вероя́тность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uslovnaja</b> verojatnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">conditional probability</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>усло́вное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выражение.html>выраже́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языке́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:программирование.html>программи́рования</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:си.html>Си</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uslovnoje</b> vyraženije v jazyke programmirovanija Si</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">a conditional expression in the C programming language</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>усло́вный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рефлекс.html>рефле́кс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uslovnyj</b> refleks</i> ― <span class="e-translation">conditioned reflex, conditioned response</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>усло́вный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>срок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uslovnyj</b> srok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">suspended sentence, probation</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>conventional <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">by convention</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>усло́вные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:символ.html>си́мволы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:элемент.html>элеме́нтов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:электрический.html>электри́ческих</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́мах</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uslovnyje</b> simvoly elementov na električeskix sxemax</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">(graphical) symbols for components in electrical schematic diagrams</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:граница.html>Грани́цы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:атмосфера.html>атмосфе́рой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>Земли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:космос.html>ко́смосом</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> Европой <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> Азией, <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>усло́вные</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:определенный.html>определены́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:однозначно.html>однозна́чно</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Granicy meždu atmosferoj Zemli i kosmosom, ili meždu Jevropoj i Azijej, vsevo lišʹ <b>uslovnyje</b>, tak kak oni ne opredeleny odnoznačno.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The boundaries between the Earth's atmosphere and outer space, or between Europe and Asia, are merely conventional, since they are not uniquely defined.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>prearranged <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">secretly agreed upon beforehand</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шпион.html>шпио́нов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>усло́вный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сигнал.html>сигна́л</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стук.html>сту́ка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U špionov byl <b>uslovnyj</b> signal: četyre stuka v dverʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The spies had a prearranged signal: four knocks on the door.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>make-believe <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pretend, imaginary, symbolic, notional, nominal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>усло́вный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:враг.html>враг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учение.html>уче́ниях</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uslovnyj</b> vrag na učenijax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the "enemy" in a war games exercise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>Усло́вная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:линия.html>ли́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>полу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разделять.html>разделя́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнату</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:половина.html>полови́ны</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Uslovnaja</b> linija na polu razdeljajet komnatu na dve poloviny.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">An imaginary line on the floor divides the room into two halves.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>reference <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a standard unit used as a basis for calculation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:условный.html>Усло́вная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:единица.html>единица</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:измерение.html>измере́ния</a> — «качественно-скорректированный <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a>».</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Uslovnaja</b> jedinica izmerenija — “kačestvenno-skorrektirovannyj god žizni”.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The reference unit of measurement is the quality-adjusted life-year (QALY).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
